  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8a85e9bd-5db6-452f-b332-976613e8e8ee'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer12016714903936087814">In BETRAYED, the second installment of the Trust series, Sophia, Ethan and Alistair will face and revisit their past dark deeds. <br/><br/>Each one of them will need to overcome their guilt, fear and pain and learn to see themselves through forgiving eyes. <br/>Or succumb to their misery.<br/><br/>Alistair Connor MacCraig, a powerful banker, and Ethan Ashford, a steel tycoon, are both in love with</span>
  <span id="freeText12016714903936087814" style="display:none">In BETRAYED, the second installment of the Trust series, Sophia, Ethan and Alistair will face and revisit their past dark deeds. <br /><br />Each one of them will need to overcome their guilt, fear and pain and learn to see themselves through forgiving eyes. <br />Or succumb to their misery.<br /><br />Alistair Connor MacCraig, a powerful banker, and Ethan Ashford, a steel tycoon, are both in love with Sophia Leibowitz, the ravishing owner of Leibowitz Oil.<br /><br />Sophia fells for Alistair's seduction. She is determined to have a relationship with him but a dark and terrible secret lurks beneath the surface she presents to the world. When she regains her memories, shame and fear will take control of her. Will she be able to find peace within herself?<br /><br />Alistair is in love with Sophia but he has difficulties overcoming his guilty over his daughter's death and his sexual preferences. Certain that he doesn't deserve to be loved, he would do everything to push Sophia away, despite his love for her. Will he be able to find redemption? <br /><br />Ethan, no less haunted by his secrets and lies, lives in an alternate reality because the loss of Sophia is too unbearable to face. He would do everything to have Sophia back in his arms.</span>

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_561555795" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/561555795" />
    <a title="Dolors" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18383778-dolors"><img alt="Dolors" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1502350013p2/18383778.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/561555795?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dolors" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dolors" href="/user/show/18383778-dolors">Dolors</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Those in for classic romance and modern erotica</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Dolors by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/14649015-poet-gentleness">Poet Gentleness</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18383778-dolors?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18383778-dolors?shelf=giveaways">giveaways</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18383778-dolors?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer561555795" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer634692561973749404">They are rich, they are young, they are attractive...but are they also doomed?<br/><i>“The mask, given time, comes to be the face itself”</i> whispers Sophia, the glamorous protagonist of this suggestive tale of love and redemption, quoting <i>Marguerite Yourcenar</i> to mercurial Alistair Connor, a fallen angel with a dark past held captive in a robust body and a puerile mind, whom she endeavors to save from himself. But is Sophia ready to be saved?<br/><br/><i>Betrayed</i> is the second installment in the <i>Trust Trilogy</i>, in which</span>
  <span id="freeText634692561973749404" style="display:none">They are rich, they are young, they are attractive...but are they also doomed?<br /><i>“The mask, given time, comes to be the face itself”</i> whispers Sophia, the glamorous protagonist of this suggestive tale of love and redemption, quoting <i>Marguerite Yourcenar</i> to mercurial Alistair Connor, a fallen angel with a dark past held captive in a robust body and a puerile mind, whom she endeavors to save from himself. But is Sophia ready to be saved?<br /><br /><i>Betrayed</i> is the second installment in the <i>Trust Trilogy</i>, in which readers who previously met Sophia and Alistair will continue to unravel their mysterious pasts, impenetrable psyches and most deeply rooted fears and to bask in the distinctive sophistication of Serruya’s high class characters who wrestle against the conventions of their frivolous lives using indestructible love as their only weapon.<br />Set in the present time and mainly a vivid romance with tinges of erotica and some erratic yet brilliant flashes of existential pondering, Serruya draws an opulent setting with steady hand that contrasts with the blurriness of disgruntled characters, whose scarred memories prevent them from showing their true colors and paint an harmonious future.<br />Traumatized rivals, ghosts of perverted ex-wives and all kind of menacing acquaintances embodying Sophia and Alistair’s past demons will try to destabilize their perfect union while disclosing themes such as the fragile line separating harmless jealousy from obsessive possession or the multiple challenges independent women in traditionally male-dominated fields are exposed to.<br />Parental relationships, psychological abuse and morbid dependency syndrome become the backdrop of a lavish scenario alternating sumptuous Scottish castles, mansions in Brazil and luxurious apartments in London.<br />Will Alistair and Sophia’s love prevail or will they succumb to their own vulnerabilities and betray what they most covet, missing their only chance for salvation? <br /><br />Cristiane Serruya offers an effective form of uncomplicated escapism with this fast paced novel that provides tantalizing entertainment and fleeting gratification sprinkled with uneven yet incisive brushstrokes of the female psyche and its most hidden desires.<br />My reading experience with erotica is far too limited to draw appropriate parallels with other writers of the same genre, but Serruya’s lavish descriptions of the Scottish landscape evoke those of Diana Gabaldon’s in her <i>“Outlander”</i> series and her refreshing prose manages to delineate the elusive concept of self-respect with firm pulse, reminding me of headstrong and dignified Claire Randall, the main character in the aforesaid series.<br />Both Sophia and Alistair might choose to remain opaque behind the masks of confidence they so carefully built to disguise their insecurities from each other, but they appear crystal clear in the eyes of the reader and even predictable in the many twists and turns, falling-in-and-outs and feverish, sometimes even overheated reconciliations that permeate the story. <br />All in all, a rewarding journey in spite of it lacking the spark of the unknown that came with the first installment, which I am sure will magically be rekindled in earnest in <i>Pandora’s Box</i>, the last volume in the <i>Trust Trilogy</i>.<br />***<br />Note: I was offered a free copy of this novel in exchange for an honest review.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="634692561973749404" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/550692023?book_show_action=true">Mar 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gigi Tous" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gigi Tous" href="/user/show/17339144-gigi-tous">Gigi Tous</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone, Anyone (15 and up)</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17339144-gigi-tous?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer550692023" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12755874877382255703">I almost always review a book the moment I finish with it but with this book I needed a couple of days to digest it in my head. <br/><br/>I went into this book expecting much, yes, and - wow! I was wrong. Betrayed is even better than A New Beginning. And it is even hotter than the first one. <br/>First, the formatting is different from the first one. Ms. Serruya takes us from present to past, back to present and then again back to the past. So many revelations and so many angst and dark scenes. Through Sophia'</span>
  <span id="freeText12755874877382255703" style="display:none">I almost always review a book the moment I finish with it but with this book I needed a couple of days to digest it in my head. <br><br>I went into this book expecting much, yes, and - wow! I was wrong. Betrayed is even better than A New Beginning. And it is even hotter than the first one. <br>First, the formatting is different from the first one. Ms. Serruya takes us from present to past, back to present and then again back to the past. So many revelations and so many angst and dark scenes. Through Sophia's, Alistair's and Ethan's past and dark secrets, much is revealed and explained.<br><br>In 555 pages, with less descriptions than the first book, as we already know the characters and their idiosyncrasies and the settings, Ms. Serruya dug deep in emotions and characters' interactions. With so many insights and so many feelings splayed and spilling through its pages, this book is a roller-coaster. It made me cry and sob with Alistair, it made me fear for Sophia's life and sanity, it made me hate Ethan and at the same time pity him, it made me laugh with Gabriela, Lachlann, Tavish and Scott. It made me happy, sad and mad. Specially at the end, it made me specially mad. This is not nice, Ms. Serruya, not nice at all. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I was so happy that Sophia and Alistair were going to marry and have their HEA and in the last sentence of the book - <b>the last sentence</b> you tell us it is not forever?! <b>Why, Ms. Serruya? Why are you so mean?</b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> But I love you anyway, Ms. Serruya. <br>It was quite astounding how Ms. Serruya leads the readers to think one thing and then bam! she leaves us all cliff-hanging again. Although it made me mad, I found that to be really, really great! <br><br>Ms. Serruya has a superb way of writing. She has an amazing talent with descriptions and does a great job twisting her words. She writes flawlessly and makes the readers feel as if a film is passing in front of their eyes. Now, Ms. Serruya, I challenge you to do an even better book than the first two installments to end this trilogy! Keep writing, keep bringing these marvelous books to us.<br>A little casting:<br>Sophia - She was very hard to find, but I guess she would be something along these lines:<br><span>[image error]</span><br>Alistair Connor is impossible. Ms. Serruya created such a handsome, amazing man, that after hours looking, this is the best I could find and still I know it's not fair to AC. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411838i/809522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>and Ethan (not so difficult to find):<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411838i/809523._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

Describing my awe to Trust's 2nd Installment is a pretty long review that no words can match it's SUPERB! <br><br>AND I HOPE THIS LOVE TRIANGLE WILL SETTLE SOONER... I HAVE MY BIAS HERE SO I'LL START CHEERING: Ethan and Sophia! Team Ethan! <br><br>At any rate...<br><br>Trust Trilogy, you won't regret having it on your bookshelf/eBook reader. <br><br>A ROMANCE LIKE NO OTHER.<br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4306654367256151341"><b>Well. Well, well, well! I wasn't expecting it!</b><br/>The first book was good, very good, <b>but this one is intelligent, deep, touching.</b> It will make you smile and laugh, it will make you cry and sad, it will make you fell good and happy. <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417523ra/825979.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>It took me on an emotional storm that left me wrung out but richer. It's beautifully crafted - every element, every character, all combined and contributing to the artful and emotionally intense world Cristiane creates. I felt caught up in, and utterly swept away by its </span>
  <span id="freeText4306654367256151341" style="display:none"><b>Well. Well, well, well! I wasn't expecting it!</b><br>The first book was good, very good, <b>but this one is intelligent, deep, touching.</b> It will make you smile and laugh, it will make you cry and sad, it will make you fell good and happy. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417523ra/825979.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>It took me on an emotional storm that left me wrung out but richer. It's beautifully crafted - every element, every character, all combined and contributing to the artful and emotionally intense world Cristiane creates. I felt caught up in, and utterly swept away by its power. <br><br>How could the second book of a trilogy, that is usually the most weak, be better than the first? For those who complained about the supposed excessive descriptions/brands on the first book (not me, by the way. I love them all), be happy, there are considering less descriptions/brands. But still the book is fashionable without being OTP. <br>The story flows smoothly and fast. It's not a story you read on a seating if you have to work on the following day. The book is huge: 555 pages of <b>intelligent reading, an intelligent hot romance</b>. You have to stop and think. Sometimes you have to go back in the book. Not because she didn't explain the scene well. <b>No.</b> Because it is so pungent, so beautiful, and so intelligent that you want to memorize every part of the book. And it will make you evaluate many thing you have done in you life. And, better, it will make you think twice before doing something.<br>Don't get me wrong! This is not a treaty or one of those boring books trying to pass on morals. While it's an intelligent book, things are hot, hot, hot too. But even on the hot scenes there're something delicate and insightful. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417523ra/825980.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The name, Betrayed, it's not what it seems. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There is no real physical betrayal on this book. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I believe it's done on purpose, to make us think that sometimes the worst betrayal is done in so many different ways that we don't even perceive it.<br><br>And dear Sophia - :O - is not what she seems too. I was astonished! I could never imagine the twist and turns Cristiane Serruya created. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401023ra/777678.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>When we meet Sophia in the first book, she is all charm, politeness and primness. Since figuring out Sophia is an enormous part of the emotionally process while she regains her memories, I won't take that away from you, not even on a spoiler parenthesis. <br><br>Instead of the first book that started a little slow this takes you on a roller-caster from the epilogue.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417523ra/825981.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The flashes of <b>Ethan's</b> early childhood, teenage and young adult years make your heart bleeds for him. Seeing it from a very realistic angle, we can understand a bit his obsession. One of the most realistic fictional characters I have read. Some people wish they had the courage to wake up one day, throw away all the bad things they have been through and realize there is more to life. I guess Ethan has tried it. But every time he starts doing this, he falls again. And he can't go anywhere, he can't get away from it all. So, he learns how to live with all his pains and betrayals and hurts. <br>Then we have hunk, tortured, Alistair that suffers and suffers and OMG suffers, as he sees flash-backs of his younger years and tells Sophia of his late wife's <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[betrayal in threesome, orgies, drugs and so much more <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br>Oh. And How could I forget dear, dear Gabriela. Intelligent, fiery loyal, Gabriela. On the chapters, she make me cry again. In fact, the three of them, Alistair, Sophia and Gabriela.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392467ra/755527.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It is hard to share much of the story without giving it away. If you thought Sophia amazing before, wait for this book. If you loved Alistair and Ethan, OMG!! read this book.<br>The characters came out much more complex and real-feeling, with their unique voices and dramas. Yes, Sophia's, Ethan's and Alistair's personas are illusions, façades that are peeled off layer by layer. <br><br>And although the end is satisfying, it still has many, many things that leaves you hanging and screaming:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/492585.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cristiane, you are now my favorite author. And I hope to be your biggest fan!<br>I'll be hibernating till Pandora's Box.<br>P.S. - A last word. Cristiane Serruya looks very much like Sophia. She is very intelligent, attentive to the details, to her readers, reviewers and friends. She is kind and polite. I'm honored to call her my favourite author.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText18019330736110130479" style="display:none">I read this book as a beta reader so I was honored with getting it ahead of schedule. WOW, WOW, WOW! That's about all I can say. <br /><br />Sophia is the perfect woman with an awesome sense of humor. She is beautiful with a sense of style and class. She stands up for herself even under the worst circumstances but it will take you by surprise how smart &amp; insightful she is. Emotionally she feels and says all the right things. She is in love with an Alpha male (Alistair) but can HER Alpha side and his strong side keep them together. Alistair's dark side forces Sophia to escape, not sure that she wants what Alistair could be offering. Alistair &amp; Sophia, both deeply in love with each other (not feeling worthy of each other but can't stay away from each other) want each other but not sure that their personalities are good together. He wants a woman to submit (Alistair likes to give orders) she doesn't want to submit (and let me tell you, she does a good job at bucking him every chance she has). It is a battle of wills between the 2 of them both physically &amp; emotionally. The sex, I can't even begin to describe that. Ethan is still in love with Sophia &amp; he will do anything he can to get her back. Then another character comes into play (Anna, Alistair's deceased wife's sister). Trouble! <br /><br />Sophia's is starting to remember. She was shot when her 1st husband was kidnapped and remembers very little of the trauma she endured during the kidnapping. She has nightmares and they are vivid and frequent. She has secrets &amp; she is not sure why anyone would love her once she reveals her sins. Alistair has his secrets too. Can they both survive together once they reveal their sins. <br /><br />I highly recommend this book. It has so much depth, story line is rich and well planned. The physical &amp; emotional content is chilling. So many parts of this book brought tears to my eyes. The descriptive content is flawless. Grab this series, you won't regret it. It is definitely a book you will want to read again. Highly emotional, Highly erotic. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16730934837620530894">Intelligent. Emotional. Romantic. Sensual. Fast. Thriller. <b>A MUST READ</b><br/><br/>It took me awhile to finish this romance because I had a business trip after I started, but I guess if I hadn't I would read it without even sleeping.<br/><br/><b>Betrayed is better than A New Beginning.</b> It's not quite that Cristiane's style has changed but it's surely more mature, flower.   <span id="freeText16730934837620530894" style="display:none">Intelligent. Emotional. Romantic. Sensual. Fast. Thriller. <b>A MUST READ</b><br><br>It took me awhile to finish this romance because I had a business trip after I started, but I guess if I hadn't I would read it without even sleeping.<br><br><b>Betrayed is better than A New Beginning.</b> It's not quite that Cristiane's style has changed but it's surely more mature, flower. The first book was good, but this... <b>Can I give it 10 golden stars?</b><br><br>It still has it's hot sex scenes - wow! but, I quite don't know how to explain, the emotions are deeper, the writing is smoother and the pace is even faster. <br><br>The story line was tragic yet beautiful. . . And differently from the first book, where Cristiane involved us in billionaire brands and places, this one is rawer. Some parts were so tragically painful that I had to stop because my tears won't let me continue. My heart broke and was put together, broke all over again and when I thought that I was mend, with just one sentence, with the last sentence before the epilogue, Cristiane broke my heart again. There weren't enough tragedies for Sophia and Alistair? <br><br>The pleasurable and painful moments were both beautifully done. The characters are so well layered so fleshed out, I felt like I knew them and I could really relate to them, even to Ethan. If you enjoy books that are character driven, deal with issues and emotions that are real, but give you hope that even the darkest times can be flooded with light, then you will love Betrayed. <br>Sophia and Ethan were so sensitively dealt, how their relationship was dealt with that I almost thought - and I still hope - that the love triangle is undone, that Ethan would have a HEA.<br>Then Alistair and Sophia's relationship was amazingly treated. I thought that they wouldn't stay together because of Alistair's BDSM preferences, and then I found myself - Wait a moment - is this considered BDSM too? <br>And although I was screaming 'say yes, say yes!!' I fully understood her doubts, her anguish and her fears. And I was in awe of the lengths Sophia went to considered staying with him.<br>My heart broke for Alistair and Nathalie and Sophia, Gabriel and Gabriela, and then it soared as Sophia and Alistair met half-way and they could have hope in life again. <br>That wonderful little girl, Gabriela, reminds me much of my own niece and how some children can be so intelligent and perceptive and help the adults through difficult ways with a simple question or gesture. A hurray for you, Gabriela.<br><br>Through the story of these three amazing characters, you will experience hurt, pain, anger, hate, fear, lust, love, hope,(among lots of others) and most importantly redemption.<br><br>OMG! That redemption scene in her TV room and the one with Gabriela almost at the end of the book was absolutely moving.<br><br>I will read anything Cristiane writes, because she gave me, in what some people would call a romance, profound messages that will stay with me forever.<br><b>This was hands down one of the most amazing books I've ever read. I'm eternally devoted!</b><br>Do not go another day without reading this book. Shove everything in your TBR pile down one, and put this on top. <br><b>You won't regret it!!</b><br><span>[image error]</span></span>

<div id="review_650370061" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/650370061" />
    <a title="Penelope" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21491391-penelope"><img alt="Penelope" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1422655696p2/21491391.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/650370061?book_show_action=true">Jun 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Penelope" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Penelope" href="/user/show/21491391-penelope">Penelope</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone over 16 </span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Penelope by: </span>
      Good reviews
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21491391-penelope?shelf=spectacular">spectacular</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer650370061" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17455560388633706930">"Trust: Betrayed" by Cristiane Serruya is the sequel of the TRUST trilogy. To say it was a wonderful read if the understatement of the century. <br/>The book itill brings to us the 'filthy rich, beautiful tormented souls' of Sophia, Ethan and Alistair, but now they revisits face to face in their pasts what caused their torments and what made them the way they are. They are struggling to see themselves through forgiving eyes, but have yet to learn how to do it. <br/>The readers are taken from present to th</span>
  <span id="freeText17455560388633706930" style="display:none">"Trust: Betrayed" by Cristiane Serruya is the sequel of the TRUST trilogy. To say it was a wonderful read if the understatement of the century. <br />The book itill brings to us the 'filthy rich, beautiful tormented souls' of Sophia, Ethan and Alistair, but now they revisits face to face in their pasts what caused their torments and what made them the way they are. They are struggling to see themselves through forgiving eyes, but have yet to learn how to do it. <br />The readers are taken from present to the past and back and forth. In a completely different writing style, but not at all boring or confusing, uch on the opposite, engaging and compelling, we are able to better understand the emotions and the depths that drive together and apart these lovers as their motives become clear and their personalities unfold, revealing secrets they are unimaginable. <br /><br />It seems a huge book (555 pages), but this novel has so many twists and turns that it moves so quickly that before you know it's over and you are starting it all over again. <br /><br />I was left thinking omg... and then wth... And then I needed a cold shower! The story line is so rich and well plotted and the physical, emotional content makes you laugh and cry, smile and cry again. <br />I love how Cristiane Serruya dug her nails in and skinned out Sophia's and Alistair Connor's dramas, by showing their compelling internalization and dilemmas. <br />The ways they went through were heart wrenching, and crawling through out of those love, dramas and choices to be made was emotionally and mentally torturous for the readers and I'm sure for the author too. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Their great love for each other is what saved them. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Cristiane Serruya wrote those sequences with heart and self-deprecation. <br />The misery, guilt, pain and fear surround the three leading main characters, who are tormented with daily and past problems are humbling. They are well-balanced, realistic and easy to relate, even with their bad flaws.<br /><br />It has a flawless descriptive content, without so many brands dropping, but still with the properly described setting that only lead the reader to one certain conclusion: "Trust: Betrayed" was a excellent amazing read.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[A P.S. - One of the scenes that had me most in tears was the one were Gabriela asks Alistair is she could call him Daddy. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />That was be not fair, that was the most beautiful thing I have ever read.<br /><br />Cristiane Serruya, as always, is a master of characterization. It's worth another read!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17455560388633706930" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_550713443" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/550713443" />
    <a title="Alberto Finamore" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17346383-alberto-finamore"><img alt="Alberto Finamore" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1360696508p2/17346383.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/550713443?book_show_action=true">Mar 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alberto Finamore" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alberto Finamore" href="/user/show/17346383-alberto-finamore">Alberto Finamore</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">First book in the series</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17346383-alberto-finamore?shelf=best-ever">best-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17346383-alberto-finamore?shelf=contemporary-erotic-romance">contemporary-erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17346383-alberto-finamore?shelf=trilogy">trilogy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17346383-alberto-finamore?shelf=books-that-make-u-think">books-that-make-u-think</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer550713443" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11056324218738314980">This is a sequel to Trust: A New Beginning, <b>and is much more better than the first.</b><br/>The second of the TRUST trilogy takes us back to the billionaire world of insanely beautiful, painfully tormented souls of Sofia, Alistair and Ethan.<br/>We are able to better understand the emotions that drive these lovers together and apart as their motives become clear and lawyers of their personalities and peeled for us. Instead of a onion, think of a rose blossoming.<br/>This adds to the compelling need to know more an</span>
  <span id="freeText11056324218738314980" style="display:none">This is a sequel to Trust: A New Beginning, <b>and is much more better than the first.</b><br />The second of the TRUST trilogy takes us back to the billionaire world of insanely beautiful, painfully tormented souls of Sofia, Alistair and Ethan.<br />We are able to better understand the emotions that drive these lovers together and apart as their motives become clear and lawyers of their personalities and peeled for us. Instead of a onion, think of a rose blossoming.<br />This adds to the compelling need to know more and experience their amazing lives from the three POV. The plot thickens and deepens, and the already complex characters reveal their dark deeds and a secrets. <br /><br />It proves that even in paradise, there are misgivings, cynicism and doubt. And no matter the privileges and wealth, <b>the rich aren't different from the rest of us.</b><br /><br />The book is very complex nonetheless extremely organized and the way it's narrated makes the complexity disappear. I enjoyed its multiple layers as they are peeled, and was not bothered by details at all. <br />And the thoughts we can hear, and the different things they say is absolutely insightful for the readers. <b>A round of applause for Cristiane.</b><br /><br />Sophia is, (after my wife) the perfect woman. She has style and class and a sense of humor. She is strong and stands up for herself, even under the worst circumstances but it will take you by surprise how smart &amp; insightful she is. She is in love with an Alpha male (Alistair) but can HER Alpha side and his strong side keep them together?<br />Sophia's is starting to remember. She was shot and developed partial amnesia very little of the trauma she endured during her husband's kidnapping. . She has secrets &amp; she is not sure why anyone would love her once she reveals her sins. Her secret is so dark, that it shocked me, But my wife (her again) said she would have done the same thing. <br /><br />Alistair has his secrets too. Alistair has secrets and although decided he can compromised he commits a fault - well two. <b>APPLAUSES FOR SOPHIA ON THE FIRST SCENE.</b><br />Can they both survive together once they reveal their sins?<br /><br />Alistair's dark side forces Sophia to escape after a later scene, she is not sure that she is ready for what Alistair wants. <br /><br />Alistair &amp; Sophia, both deeply in love with each other, are afraid of not feeling worthy of each other because of their secrets. Nonetheless, they can't stay away from each other. There's a battle of wills, physically &amp; emotionally. Can too Alpha partners co-exists? <br /><br />Ethan is still in love with Sophia &amp; he will do anything he can to get her back. As much as I want to hate Ethan, even his anger, fear and doubt is reasoned in his mistreat, neglected and abused childhood. <br /><br />Then another character comes into play (Emma, Alistair's deceased wife's sister). Trouble in sight! Will their love survive another trouble?<br /><br />I highly recommend this book. It's physical &amp; emotional content. So many parts of this book brought tears my wife's eyes. It has so much depth, it's fat paced and story line is rich and well planned. It's flawless. Grab this series, you won't regret it. Highly emotional, Highly erotic. The sex, I can't even begin to describe that. It's not erotica, it's subtle and it enhances their relationship. <br />I enjoyed this book (and my wife much more, she asked me to say this.) It is definitely a book you will want to read again and put on your favorite shelf (or kindle)<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11056324218738314980" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer765539057" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15427404942721125255">Trust Betrayed( Part-2 of the Trust Series)<br/><br/>'Widowed were not those alive, but those who were dead.'- Cristiane Serruya<br/><br/>Some secrets are revealed, some hearts broken and many dreams will come true... or atleast they should!<br/><br/>This is a journey worth embarking upon by all adults atleast once, because it has so much more than what is considered to be the staple content in all romantic fictions. It is a tragedy yet a tale of hope, of happiness, regrets and a never-ending suspense and above all, a melanc</span>
  <span id="freeText15427404942721125255" style="display:none">Trust Betrayed( Part-2 of the Trust Series)<br /><br />'Widowed were not those alive, but those who were dead.'- Cristiane Serruya<br /><br />Some secrets are revealed, some hearts broken and many dreams will come true... or atleast they should!<br /><br />This is a journey worth embarking upon by all adults atleast once, because it has so much more than what is considered to be the staple content in all romantic fictions. It is a tragedy yet a tale of hope, of happiness, regrets and a never-ending suspense and above all, a melancholy that stays with the reader long after the story is over.<br /><br />Guess it's the author's stint with law as a lawyer who specializes in cases of sexual abuse and violence against children and women has brought immense depth and has provided a strong foundation to this story. It brings to light many of the silent tortures that women often have to deal with and sometimes do get used to it to such an extent that they become addicted to it and it ultimately destroys their lives. <br /> <br />Some might ask- What can possibly be achieved by reading an erotic fiction except for some noxious pleasure to the reader? And to them I say – for once, try not to read the book in a shallow manner and instead venture just a bit deeper. Surely the incidents revealed to the world might not have been conjured up from thin air. <br /><br />For a 20 year old Indian reader, it did prove to be an eyeball rolling experience once in a while but then on the whole, I was mesmerized by the characters. Sophia, a widow with Gabriela, her daughter, Alistair and Ethan, both fighting their inner devils and changed by the circumstances that life sometimes offers (mind you, it can be so much worse than we think it is possible!) Delve a little deeper and the personality of Tavish can leave you spell-bound. Lachlanne, Alice, Leonard- I could go on and on about all of them. I would gladly give 6-stars for the characterization part alone.<br /><br />For a so-called philosophical being like me, I did get more and more pulled into the way the world functions, one’s destiny and inner-turmoil, the desperate attempts to flee from one’s own past only to be caught red-handed by some memories thrown onto your face when you least expect them to. <br /><br />As a reader, one gets the exclusive opportunity to relish picturesque places (only a well-travelled author can present something like this) and regale one’s senses in the exquisite emotions that are Godsend in all human beings which is packed in this book. Don’t forget to read the Part-1 of the book before turning pages of this one (‘Trust’ me- it would be more beautiful that way). <br /><br />For review of Part-1 of the Trust Series- <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://critiquedontcriticize.blogspot.in/2013/09/trust-new-beginning-book-review.html">http://critiquedontcriticize.blogspot...</a><br /><br />Time for Pandora’s Box (Part-3 of the Trust Series). <br /><br />Cristiane, Trust - Encore!<br /><br />-Divya Nambiar<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16160314.Trust_A_New_Beginning__Trust___1_" title="Trust A New Beginning (Trust, #1) by Cristiane Serruya" rel="nofollow noopener">Trust: A New Beginning</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17454163.Trust_Betrayed__Trust___2_" title="Trust Betrayed (Trust, #2) by Cristiane Serruya" rel="nofollow noopener">Trust: Betrayed</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17801272.Trust_Pandora_s_Box__Trust___3_" title="Trust Pandora's Box (Trust, #3) by Cristiane Serruya" rel="nofollow noopener">Trust: Pandora's Box</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17982897.The_Modern_Man_A_philosophical_divagation_about_the_evil_banality_of_daily_acts" title="The Modern Man A philosophical divagation about the evil banality of daily acts by Cristiane Serruya" rel="nofollow noopener">The Modern Man: A philosophical divagation about the evil banality of daily acts</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6583811.Cristiane_Serruya" title="Cristiane Serruya" rel="nofollow noopener">Cristiane Serruya</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15427404942721125255" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText11863582789409066120" style="display:none">THIS BOOK WAS AWESOME!!!!<br /><br />We get to know more about Sophia's, Alistair's and Ethan's past, I really liked that because now I can understand them better <b>BUT</b> I didn't like when I was reading a <b>REALLY REALLY REALLY</b> good scene or someone was going to say something important and <b>BOOM</b> a scene from the past!! Not cool!!<br /><br />I really really like Sophia!!! Alistair tries to order her around and she's like : "oh I don't think so!!" and does the opposite :D There was one thing I didn't like about her in this book SHE SAID SHE TRUSTS HIM BUT DOESN'T TELL HIM HER SECRETS!!!! While she pressures Alistair to tell her his secrets which he tells her because he knew that his ex wife was getting in the way of his relationship with her!! I was REALLY surprised when I discovered Sophia's secret I was like WOW REALLY?!<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Sophia ordering to cut the left finger of the guys that killed Gabriel and then only one of them survived!! I totally understand where her guilt comes from, she indirectly killed 10(damn I don't remember how many guys were :/) and they had families so she "killed" fathers, husbands, brothers, etc..she lost Gabriel so she knows what the women in those man lives felt like and that's why I think she feels so guilty  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> But I think I was kinda of expecting something like that.<br /><br />Alistair Alistair *sighs* I LOVE HIM!!!!!! HE'S PERFECT FOR SOPHIA!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! (I think you know what team I am.)<br />I was so sad when I was reading the chapters that had his past!! My poor baby!!! I already knew somethings from the first book but in this one we discover EVERYTHING (I hope) <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[God having a wife like Heather jesus I want to resurrect her and kill her all over again!!!!!!!! WHAT A FREAKING BITCH !! SHE DESTROYED ALISTAIR!! Because of her he feels guilty that the night her and Natalie died he didn't call Alice first to see if his daughter was there BECAUSE OF HER HE LOST HIS ONLY DAUGHTER!!!!!! BECAUSE OF HER HE'S STERILE!!!!! I hope there's a small chance he can get Sophia pregnant!! He would be so so so happy!!!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Alistair grew a lot in this book, he accepted his past and he was finally ready to built a future with Sophia <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I WAS SO HAPPY WHEN THEY GOT ENGAGED AND THEIR WEDDING WAS SO PRETTY!!!!!!!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.I still think he overreacts sometimes but I still love him :D<br /><br />Now Ethan...I just don't understand how can people be team Ethan!!!!! God he's so OBSESSED with Sophia!! He tracks her down every freaking minute of the day!!! He hired someone to hack her computer and the place she works!!!!!!!!!! He's creepy and I pity him...yeah he had a bad past but what he does it's too much and he should find help!!!!!!!!!!! Though I don't think he's good for Sophia I still want him to have a happy ending and PLEASE don't do any crazy shit to ruin Alistair and Sophia's relationship in the third book!!!<br /><br />In this book Heather's sister shows up, Emma, and OMG BITCH!!! I will murder you!! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I WANT TO KNOW WHO WAS THE PERSON IN THE CAR WHEN SHE GOT OUT OF THE HOSPITAL!!!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Gabriel's parents also show up and let me tell you I have a bad feeling about Gabriel's father....I HATE HIM!! HE LEFT HIS SON TO DIE!!!!!!!!!!!!<br /><br />Alistair and Gabriela's relationship *-* SO SO SO ADORABLE!!! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Gabriela asking if she could call Alistair daddy!!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> god I melted when I read this part!!!<br /><br />I really enjoyed reading the second book it was much better than the first one and I can't wait to read the last book!!<br /></span>

<div id="review_740351371" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/740351371" />
    <a title="Susie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8269809-susie"><img alt="Susie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600088651p2/8269809.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/740351371?book_show_action=true">Oct 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Susie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Susie" href="/user/show/8269809-susie">Susie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/18760372-trust">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Susie by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/14649015-poet-gentleness">Poet Gentleness</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8269809-susie?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8269809-susie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8269809-susie?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8269809-susie?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8269809-susie?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8269809-susie?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer740351371" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8156676758706104739">So, my review... Ooooh, I should let it all hang, simmer, be a bit evil and let Cristiane wait a bit longer just like she does us with all those scenes...! ;)<br/><br/>Hmmm, this was somewhat slower than I'd hoped in reading, with all my eye problems, but I got there in the end. I'm glad not so many use pure white pages nowadays, or it might have taken longer!<br/><br/>But, here it comes – my completely honest review.<br/><br/>Now, as I've said before, I've never really been a fan of the genre. Erotica has always seemed a bi</span>
  <span id="freeText8156676758706104739" style="display:none">So, my review... Ooooh, I should let it all hang, simmer, be a bit evil and let Cristiane wait a bit longer just like she does us with all those scenes...! ;)<br /><br />Hmmm, this was somewhat slower than I'd hoped in reading, with all my eye problems, but I got there in the end. I'm glad not so many use pure white pages nowadays, or it might have taken longer!<br /><br />But, here it comes – my completely honest review.<br /><br />Now, as I've said before, I've never really been a fan of the genre. Erotica has always seemed a bit too sordid for me, something trying to give you what you should have in a relationship, anyway. Why do people need it? Isn't it like literary porn? Yet, I'm glad I got into this series. This is something that's far more than a quick sexual thrill, a peek beneath the sheets; this has bounds of intelligence inside its pages. What could so easily be a fuckfest of the rich, has thoughts and consequences flowing through each page. These people aren't just rich and famous, but are also thoughtful, intelligent, and realise the true worth of others.<br /><br />But the thing I loved most was that here is a woman in charge of her own destiny. Not only does she now own a company, but she is domineering, strong willed. She can say <b>”NO”</b>. That is so refreshing to see in a world filled with women being thrown about as the playthings for men. She doesn’t use them and they don’t use her. This book is about mutual respect, love, pleasure and consent. CONSENT!! Yes, you people in love with Fifty Shades of Grey and such like – did you forget that that word existed?!<br /><br />Yes, the sexual exploits perhaps go to a point that I wouldn’t, but the partner in these scenarios (notice I’m not saying which one?! :P) show such concern and respect that they allow Sophia to go where she wants to, to choose her own limits. <i>Every</i> woman deserves a partner like that!<br /><br />I also love some of the secrets that are revealed here<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ oooh, I knew that Edward had to be gay! Boy is Alistair going to be relieved when he finds out! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. And yes, I pity Ethan, for all that he’s been through, but in answer to the question I don’t think I’d accept his offer right now, as I don’t think I could be the one to fix him<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[. He’s broken, too broken. Maybe if he thought to go to a therapist as well as Alistair, there’d be a chance for him to find someone special. It’s so obvious that the abuse has had its toll on him. I don’t blame his grandfather for what happened, as he had only Ethan’s interests at heart and wanted to make him a man. But his grandfather didn’t even see that the abuse Ethan had already seen meant that his “gifts” could make things worse as well as better <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br />One thing I also found intriguing - for an ARC copy, this had so few typos compared to the last one. Yet there was a really funny one in there: "cheery threes" instead of "cherry trees". Oh dear, did that hurt to laugh!<br /><br />Now, when’s the next one?!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9781499280764959927">Exceptional! This is a book that will make you think. Think about you have read before and liked. Think about how a woman should behave. How a man should behave. And how naive you should be with your so-called friends.<br/>Apart from the hot, hot, hot scenes, there are exceptional scenes with therapists that are wonderful profound. You don't need to be what the others want you to be. You don't need to fear or to face the bad things that happened in your life. On the other hand, you MUST do it to have</span>
  <span id="freeText9781499280764959927" style="display:none">Exceptional! This is a book that will make you think. Think about you have read before and liked. Think about how a woman should behave. How a man should behave. And how naive you should be with your so-called friends.<br />Apart from the hot, hot, hot scenes, there are exceptional scenes with therapists that are wonderful profound. You don't need to be what the others want you to be. You don't need to fear or to face the bad things that happened in your life. On the other hand, you MUST do it to have a better life and to admit others in it.<br />I'm in awe. If the first book was a great romance, this one is much more than that.<br />It made me cry, it made me angry, it made me happy, it made me think.<br />Read it. You won't regret.</span>

<div id="review_588003681" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/588003681" />
    <a title="Aurora" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5726598-aurora"><img alt="Aurora" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1367732391p2/5726598.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/588003681?book_show_action=true">Apr 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aurora" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aurora" href="/user/show/5726598-aurora">Aurora</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer588003681" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17916581480746178697">Name of Book: Trust: Betrayed<br/><br/>Author: Cristiane Serruya<br/><br/>ISBN: 9781482586473<br/><br/>Publisher: Createspace<br/><br/>Part of a Series: Trust Trilogy<br/><br/>Type of book: relationships, trust, past, 1980s, 2010, love triangle, history, possession, sexuality, wealth, Scotland, Brazil, "Avenging Angel", BDSM, vanilla sex<br/><br/>Year it was published: 2013<br/><br/>Summary:<br/><br/> In BETRAYED, the second installment of the Trust series, Sophia, Ethan and Alistair will face and revisit their past dark deeds. <br/> Each one of them will need to overcome their </span>
  <span id="freeText17916581480746178697" style="display:none">Name of Book: Trust: Betrayed<br /><br />Author: Cristiane Serruya<br /><br />ISBN: 9781482586473<br /><br />Publisher: Createspace<br /><br />Part of a Series: Trust Trilogy<br /><br />Type of book: relationships, trust, past, 1980s, 2010, love triangle, history, possession, sexuality, wealth, Scotland, Brazil, "Avenging Angel", BDSM, vanilla sex<br /><br />Year it was published: 2013<br /><br />Summary:<br /><br /> In BETRAYED, the second installment of the Trust series, Sophia, Ethan and Alistair will face and revisit their past dark deeds. <br /> Each one of them will need to overcome their guilt, fear and pain and learn to see themselves through forgiving eyes. <br /> Or succumb to their misery.<br /> Alistair Connor MacCraig, a powerful banker, and Ethan Ashford, a steel tycoon, are both in love with Sophia Leibowitz, the ravishing owner of Leibowitz Oil.<br /> Sophia fells for Alistair's seduction. She is determined to have a relationship with him but a dark and terrible secret lurks beneath the surface she presents to the world. When she regains her memories, shame and fear will take control of her. Will she be able to find peace within herself?<br /> Alistair is in love with Sophia but he has difficulties overcoming his guilty over his daughter's death and his sexual preferences. Certain that he doesn't deserve to be loved, he would do everything to push Sophia away, despite his love for her. Will he be able to find redemption? <br /> Ethan, no less haunted by his secrets and lies, lives in an alternate reality because the loss of Sophia is too unbearable to face. He would do everything to have Sophia back in his arms<br /><br />Characters:<br /><br /> How many licks does it take to the center of the Tootsie Roll? My reply would be G-d only knows. How many layers does Sophia have? G-d only knows. If you think you have fully discovered Sophia in the first book, boy you are wrong. Cristiane masterfully adds more and more layers to her, many I hadn't expected. In the first book I found her an adorable and strong woman who seems to be perfect in every way. In this book we see her vulnerabilities and her dark secrets began to pop out. Perhaps she might be dealing with PTSD (Post traumatic Stress Disorder, I am thinking.) We also see more of her family members; the strong and loyal Felipe, her twin sisters who finish each other sentences, and her younger sister Carolina who has a mysterious fiancé. Alistair undergoes through a lot of changes in the book and I no longer hated him but wanted him to have a happy ending. While Ethan is there as well, we do learn a lot of his past and he was not a very active character as Sophia and Alistair and were. Gabriella and Alistair's family were there too (Am hoping for a character sheet near the future to keep all the family members straight...)<br /><br />Theme:<br /><br /> Its possible to heal through love<br /><br />Plot:<br /><br /> This is written in third person narrative from Alistair's, Ethan's and Sophia's points of view. Just like in previous book the narration moves from Alistair's to Sophia's thoughts and so forth, but perhaps I am familiar with her writing style (at least from the first book,) the style didn't annoy me. Lack of transitions between past and present scenes did annoy me, however and I almost didn't give it five stars. That annoyance did last in beginning only, and towards the middle and end the flashbacks came with transitions. One question that I am curious to ask about is, what are the color of Sophia's eyes? Are they hazel, golden or brown? (Sophia's eyes are always described as either hazel or golden...) There aren't a lot of mention of luxury brands in the book and its very tightly woven and has more action than the first book.<br /><br />Author Information:<br /> (from goodreads.com)<br /><br /> born<br /> in Rio de Janeiro, Brazil April 25, 1970 <br /><br /> gender<br /> female<br /><br /> website<br /> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://cristianeserruya.com.br">http://cristianeserruya.com.br</a> <br /><br /> twitter username<br /> CrisSerruya <br /><br /> genre<br /> Contemporary, Romance, Chick Lit <br /><br /> influences<br /> Classic literature, historical romance <br /><br /> member since<br /> November 2012<br /><br /> I live in Rio de Janeiro, Brazil, with my husband and two daughters. I'm a lawyer, who specializes in cases of sexual abuse and violence against children and women. I also have a Masters in Business Law and a BA in Fine Arts. <br /><br /> I've always loved to read, write and listen to music. I lived and studied in England, France, Italy and Switzerland. Traveling is one of my passions - as is keeping fit and healthy. <br /><br /> After twenty-two years of practicing law, I decided to give writing a go. And - amazingly - it was just the piece that was missing in my life.<br /><br />Opinion:<br /><br /> Wow, she has done it again, earned 5 stars on my book review blog. This is as good, if not better than the first book; Sophia is still smart and sexy and puts limits on herself and others; Alistair is struggling with accepting forgiveness; Ethan is absent for 98 percent of the book, although he does make appearances and the reader is treated to his history, just as more about Sophia and Alistair is also revealed. If one found the labels annoying, (I didn't, but in case if you did,) then they barely appear in this book, and its more plot driven than before. I also learned to like Alistair and rooted for him almost all the time. (Sorry Ethan,) however I did have a few problems with the book: one is to pay careful attention to the ending date in the first book before reading the second book, (in second book without a warning we are transported to few weeks after a certain event in first book,) and second thing that bothered me are the past scenes without rhyme or reason and lack of transitional words to make it smooth. For example, one scene would be focused on Sophia and Alistair, but then without a transit or mention of why, we are switched to a scene from Ethan's past (She does warn ahead of time, but it doesn't fit the narrative,) these switches really bugged me the first half of the book though. When I was done with it, I groaned to heavens at the fact I have to wait SEVEN MONTHS to hopefully read the last book!<br /><br />Quick notes: I would like to thank the author for the opportunity to read and review the book.<br /><br /> 5 out of 5<br /> (0: Stay away unless a masochist 1: Good for insomnia 2: Horrible but readable; 3: Readable and quickly forgettable, 4: Good, enjoyable 5: Buy it, keep it and never let it go.)<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://sveta-randomblog.blogspot.com/2013/05/e-reading-book-review-of-2-trust.html">http://sveta-randomblog.blogspot.com/...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="17916581480746178697" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_789530122" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/789530122" />
    <a title="Mrs." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26577559-mrs"><img alt="Mrs." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1386962440p2/26577559.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/789530122?book_show_action=true">Dec 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mrs." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mrs." href="/user/show/26577559-mrs">Mrs.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Everyone +16</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Mrs. by: </span>
      Good reviews
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26577559-mrs?shelf=exceptional">exceptional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26577559-mrs?shelf=first-reads">first-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer789530122" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15835884965892623551">So... This is the hardest time for me. <br/>When I love a book so much, it became full of highlights, it is difficult to put pen on paper to express all the fierce emotions it brought out on me. Betrayed is one of those rare books.<br/><br/>First, I must say this book has a very interesting style of going back in time, <i>exactly</i> as I needed more explanation on an obscure behavior of a character. <br/>This new (?) style of Cristiane is so gripping that it made me plunge deep in the life of her characters. It wasn't th</span>
  <span id="freeText15835884965892623551" style="display:none">So... This is the hardest time for me. <br />When I love a book so much, it became full of highlights, it is difficult to put pen on paper to express all the fierce emotions it brought out on me. Betrayed is one of those rare books.<br /><br />First, I must say this book has a very interesting style of going back in time, <i>exactly</i> as I needed more explanation on an obscure behavior of a character. <br />This new (?) style of Cristiane is so gripping that it made me plunge deep in the life of her characters. It wasn't the narrator telling me facts for afar. Her characters where telling me what happened to them, in a show-and-tell so interesting - and different from what I have read so far - that Cristiane opened their hearts and souls to me.<br />In fact, she bares her characters of all the layers of richness and aloofness that covered them in the first book. <br />Sophia, Ethan &amp; AC are still absurdly wealthy, but they have become even more human, with red (hot) blood running in their veins (in spite of AC's peerage heritage, he is the most red-hot-bloody character, imo). Their tragedies, triumphs and emotions are so real and palpable, I felt I knew them as their secrets were revealed more and more. <br /><br />Sophia is strong-willed, beautiful, has a witty sense of humor and intelligent with a loving heart. With all those highlights, her secret will shock you when it is revealed. (Although I was shocked, I understood it.) I love that she put AC in his place. She needed it and he, more than her, needed it. <br />AC, oh, Alistair Connor is the perfect blend of domineering and gentle, he takes, but he gives so much in return. He has a dark and sad past and tries hard to get rid of it. A hot Highlander.<br />Gabriela is the perfect daughter every mother (and father) wish to have.<br />And poor, dear Ethan has started to find his way to my heart. <br /><br />Sophia recovers her memory and finds Alistair’s secret wardrobe. <br />Oooooh! I almost screamed when Ethan came back into the scene. At that point I was so sure he was out of his league with Sophia and had moved on with her “generic”. That was quite a twist. But many more were waiting for me.<br />I will not spoil this review telling you about the many twists-&amp;-turns this book has. <br />I was left gaping, I cried with Sophia and Alistair, I pitied Ethan; I laughed with Gabriela; I screamed with Ethan’s abhorrent parents and I marveled with the deep insights and comments Cristiane smears the book with.<br /><br />Just when I thought everything was going to be all right, a few of the secondary characters, who were just back-ground scenario, come to the fore and threaten the HEA Cristiane waved under my nose.<br /><br />There are so many special scenes that I cannot - will not - choose one, risking changing my mind and coming back to edit this review. The whole book is special. It’s perfect, I must say.<br /><br />Cristiane does an excellent job and kept me turning the pages, craving for the next twist, for her next beautiful words, comments on daily life using classic literature, savoir-faire, psychological insights; the music, places, restaurants and the descriptions are absolutely flawless. <br />This book is flawless. <br />It has so much depth, plot is so rich and well planned; the physical &amp; emotional content is thrilling that I felt it was over before it began. So I went back to the first page and - HAPPILY - started it all over again.<br /><br />Last, but not least, I cannot finish this review without saying that the sex scenes are hot and steamy but full of love and meaning, written in such a way that it shows off the true feelings of the partners involved (or not involved) and not only the physical aspects of them.<br /><br />Betrayed brought tears to my eyes and warmth to my heart. I highly recommend this book. You won’t regret the time you’ll spend with Cristiane’s characters.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15835884965892623551" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_896335616" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/896335616" />
    <a title="John Hennessy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6981944-john-hennessy"><img alt="John Hennessy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598813178p2/6981944.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/896335616?book_show_action=true">Mar 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="John Hennessy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="John Hennessy" href="/user/show/6981944-john-hennessy">John Hennessy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6981944-john-hennessy?shelf=2014">2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer896335616" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer264886429036703719">TRUST: A New Beginning was a revelation to me in the sense that I didn't usually read these kind of stories. However, Cristiane Serruya is an excellent author, and you could tell that A New Beginning was something special.It starts with quite a bang and amazingly, keeps it up through out. That's not easy for a long book like TRUST.<br/><br/>As with any 'middle story' the trick is, could it be better than the first and yet end in a way that would set things up for a tantalising finale (I have bought TRUST:</span>
  <span id="freeText264886429036703719" style="display:none">TRUST: A New Beginning was a revelation to me in the sense that I didn't usually read these kind of stories. However, Cristiane Serruya is an excellent author, and you could tell that A New Beginning was something special.It starts with quite a bang and amazingly, keeps it up through out. That's not easy for a long book like TRUST.<br /><br />As with any 'middle story' the trick is, could it be better than the first and yet end in a way that would set things up for a tantalising finale (I have bought TRUST: Pandora's Box but am yet to review it) and I need to explain why I haven't gotten around to reading the final book yet.<br /><br />TRUST Betrayed is a complex, luxuriously layered and woven tale that is brilliantly written, but for me, I needed to re-read certain scenes just to make sure I had absorbed what had happened and take it all in. In that sense, it is the harder read than A New Beginning but is totally worth investing your time on this story.<br /><br />It's a lovely way Cristiane has with words - the date and time stamps add increased authenticity to the tale and whilst the main characters Sophia and Alistair remain as compelling as ever, it's the truly 'unique' Heather who stuck in my mind long after I had finished the story. I won't say whether Heather is good, bad or indifferent, but she adds her unique spin to the story.<br /><br />The story probably works best with all three read together, and so I'm looking forward to Pandora's Box. To date, there's only one trilogy of books that received five stars from me - Lord of the Rings. Now I know that's not an official trilogy, but the idea of rating them is the same...I rated Lotr 5 stars as a whole. Let's just say that Cristiane Serruya is a modern, intelligent writer who deserves the plaudits for her stories. Both TRUST books are excellent and I can heartily recommend them. <br /><br />In the sense of balance, is there any thing to fault? Perhaps yes, perhaps no, depending on your view. For me, Betrayed had so much going on, it deserved more than one read to really absorb it, but it is, as I say, worth your time. A light read this is not...prepare to give it the time and space it deserves, and I am sure that you too will enjoy this utterly thrilling story.<br /><br />As for book three, Pandora's Box is an awesome, intriguing title. Some books are worth waiting for, an just like Doctor Sleep by Stephen King, I waited some months before finally reading it..even for the master of horror, following up The Shining would be impossible, surely?<br /><br />Trust Betrayed is a lot like that....give some space between Book One and Book Three and I am sure you will love the ride!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="264886429036703719" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1080544417" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1080544417" />
    <a title="Lori" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5362508-lori"><img alt="Lori" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1452195034p2/5362508.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1080544417?book_show_action=true">Oct 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lori" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lori" href="/user/show/5362508-lori">Lori</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>
